beginSubroutine: s32'CheckVoiceFunc'
  returnValue: 0, 0
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(0)
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'bed'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'bed'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei'
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'pot'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'pot', 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'fau'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'fau', 0, 0
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'WFree_KobetsuFunc'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_AXL', 2, 157
  ifOperation: (AND), Mem(TrainingValue), Mem(IsMainPlayerSelf)
    if: Mem(IsRecoverableTypeA)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(600)
      checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'OneVision_Add'
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal1)
          isObjectActive: (STACK0)
          ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
            if: Mem(BattleDoing)
              createObjectWithArg: s32'axl501_Aura', (PLAYER)
              stackObject: (STACK0), (PREVIOUS)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(PlayerVal0)
    ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
      if: Mem(BattleDoing)
        ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
          ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
            modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(-2)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:
